        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>

          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21.) What airport is located approximately 47 (degrees) 40 (minutes) N latitude and 101 (degrees) 26 (minutes) W longitude?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Garrison Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Mercer County Regional Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Semshenko Airport.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Under what condition should the operator of a small UA establish scheduled maintenance protocol?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  When the FAA requires you to, following an accident.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  UAS does not need a required maintenance schedule.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  When the manufacturer does not provide a maintenance schedule.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 2.) If an unmanned airplane weighs 33 pounds, what approximate weight would the airplane structure be required to support during a 30� banked turn while maintaining altitude?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_2/main-08aec798e611ae97212586f5e0fb9366d877818523df8aaba1a75f1c8597b872.png">Figure 2</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  47 pounds.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  34 pounds.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  38 pounds.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What effect does high density altitude have on the efficiency of a UA propeller?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Propeller efficiency is increased.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  Propeller efficiency is decreased.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  Density altitude does not affect propeller efficiency.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>As a remote-pilot operating near an airport, you should expect arriving aircraft to join the traffic pattern</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>

                </label>
              </div>

                  overflying the runway and turning downwind
                </label>

        <h1>Questions 6&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;10</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What are characteristics of a moist, unstable air mass?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Poor visibility and smooth air.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratiform clouds and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Cumuliform clouds and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What are the characteristics of stable air?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Poor visibility and steady precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Good visibility and steady precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Poor visibility and intermittent precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21, area 2.) What is the floor of controlled airspace along V15?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/area_2-f6dcdf188614931df67f59b71f4ad4a05b0839255d29c45f3c25813450e308ed.png">Figure 21 - Area 2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Refer to the Chart Supplements
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  14,500 ft MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  1200 ft AGL
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What effect does high density altitude have on the efficiency of a UA propeller?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Density altitude does not affect propeller efficiency.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  Propeller efficiency is decreased.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  Propeller efficiency is increased.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which would most likely result in hyperventilation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  An extremely slow rate of breathing and insufficient oxygen.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="true">
                  Emotional tension, anxiety, or fear.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  The excessive consumption of alcohol.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

        <h1>Questions 11&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;15</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>

      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 2.) The floor of Class B airspace at Addison Airport is</h3>

                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/area2-075d3f95fa650447df66f4db7be9a4f3ff0cb980b777463f18740610123dd856.png">Figure 25 - Area2</a></li>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 16&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;20</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Within how many days must an sUAS accident be reported to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  10 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  90 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  30 days
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You are part of a news crew, operating an sUAS to cover a breaking story. You experience a flyaway during landing. The unmanned aircraft strikes a vehicle, causing approximately $800 worth of damage. When must you report the accident to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  If requested
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Within 30 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  Within 10 days
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 107, the responsibility to inspect the small UAS to ensure it is in a safe operating condition rests with the</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  visual observer.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  owner of the small UAS
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  remote pilot-in-command.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 2.) The control tower frequency for Addison Airport is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/main-57bc6a20997504c7dfe6d1e894e7811561453c502faadd4248a5f29a8ea0c65e.png">Figure 25</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/area2-075d3f95fa650447df66f4db7be9a4f3ff0cb980b777463f18740610123dd856.png">Figure 25 - Area2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  133.4 MHz
                </label>

    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 21&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;25</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When loading cameras or other equipment on an sUAS, mount the items in a manner that</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Is visible to the visual observer or other crewmembers.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  Does not adversly affect the center of gravity.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Can be easily removed without the use of tools.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which crewmember must hold a remote pilot certificate with an sUAS rating?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  The person manipulating the controls
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  The visual observer (VO)
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  The Remote Pilot in Command (Remote PIC)
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 15) In the TAF for KMEM, what does SHRA stand for?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  A shift in wind deriction is expected
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  A significant change in precipitation is possible
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  Rain Showers
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>A local TV station has hired a remote pilot to operate their small UA to cover breaking news stories. The remote pilot has had multiple near misses with obstacles on the ground and two small UAS accidents. What would be a solution for the news station to improve their operating safety culture?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">
                  The news station should recognize hazardous attitudes and situations and develop standard operating procedures that emphasize safety.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  The news station does not need to make any changes; there are times that an accident is unavoidable.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  The news station should implement a policy of no more than five crashes/incidents within 6 months.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the purpose of the rudder on an airplane?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  To control yaw
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  To control roll
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  To control overbanking tendency
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

        <h1>Questions 26&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;30</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Responsibility for collision avoidance in controlled airspace rests with</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Air Traffic Control
                </label>
              </div>

                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  all pilots
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  the controlling agency
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) Who would a Remote Pilot in Command contact to &quot;CHECK NOTAMS&quot; as it is noted in the CAUTION box regarding the unmarked balloon?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  NTSB office
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="true">
                  Flight Service
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  FAA district office
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>To avoid striking guy wires, how far from a skeletal tower shoud you operate your aircraft?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  500 feet
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>

                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  1000 feet
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">

                </label>

                </label>

                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  The visual observer (VO)
                </label>
              </div>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 31&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;35</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>While operating a small unmanned aircraft system (sUAS), you experience a flyaway and several people suffer injuries. Which of the following injuries requires reporting to the FAA?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Scrapes and cuts bandaged on site
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Minor bruises
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  An injury requiring a hospitalization over 48 hours
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 15) What is the valid period for the TAF for KMEM?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  2200Z to 1600Z
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  1700Z to 2000Z
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  1800Z to 2400Z
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>To get a complete weather overview for the planned flight, the Remote Pilot in Command should obtain a</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  An abbreviated briefing
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  An outlook briefing
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  A standard briefing
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21.) You have been hired by a farmer to use your small UA to inspect his crops. The area that you are to survey is in the Devil`s Lake West MOA, east of area 2. How would you find out if the MOA is active?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Locate the information in the Small UAS database.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  Contact Flight Service
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  Refer to the Military Operations Directory.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You are a remote pilot for a co-op energy service provider. You are to use your UA to inspect power lines in a remote area 15 hours away from your home office. After the drive, fatigue impacts your abilities to complete your assignment on time. Fatigue can be recognized</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  as being in an impaired state.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  easily by an experienced pilot.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  by an ability to overcome sleep deprivation.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">

          </div>

                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="true">
                  Yes, this is a Military Training Route from 1,500 feet AGL and below.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  Yes, the defined route provides traffic separation to manned aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">
            <button type="submit" id="faa_submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg btn-block">Grade my responses</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>

        <h1>Questions 41&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;45</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) Who would a Remote Pilot in Command contact to &quot;CHECK NOTAMS&quot; as it is noted in the CAUTION box regarding the unmarked balloon?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  FAA district office
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">

    </div>
    <div class="col-sm-9">
      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 46&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;50</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When requesting a waiver, the required documents should be presented to the FAA at least how many days prior to the planned operation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  10 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="true">
                  90 days
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  30 days
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 48, when must a person register a small UA with the Federal Aviation Administration?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  All civilian small UAs weighing greater than .55 pounds must be registered regardless of its intended use.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  When the small UA is used for any purpose other than as a model aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Only when the operator will be paid for commercial services.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Damaged lithium batteries can cause</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Increased endurance
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">
                  An inflight fire
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  A change in aircraft center of gravity
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Between 1000Z and 1200Z the visibility at KMEM is forecast to be?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  1 SM
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  1/2 SM
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  3 SM
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 107 the remote pilot-in-command (PIC) of a small unmanned aircraft planning to operate within Class C airspace</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  must use a visual observer.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  is required to file a flight plan.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  is required to receive ATC authorization.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

        <h1>Questions 51&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;55</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>If an unstable air mass is forced upward, what type clouds can be expected?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Clouds with considerable vertical development and associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with little vertical development.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with considerable associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Who is ultimately responsible for preventing a hazardous situation before an accident occurs?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  The person manipulating the controls
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="true">
                  The Remote Pilot in Command (Remote PIC)
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  The visual observer (VO)
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 66&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;70</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which would most likely result in hyperventilation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  Emotional tension, anxiety, or fear.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  The excessive consumption of alcohol.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  An extremely slow rate of breathing and insufficient oxygen.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What are the characteristics of stable air?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Poor visibility and steady precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Good visibility and steady precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Poor visibility and intermittent precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Responsibility for collision avoidance in controlled airspace rests with</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="true">
                  all pilots
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  the controlling agency
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  Air Traffic Control
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 21.) You have been hired by a farmer to use your small UA to inspect his crops. The area that you are to survey is in the Devil`s Lake West MOA, east of area 2. How would you find out if the MOA is active?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_21/main-310f135d42123ac9656452743e4d40276598dbb31a45d091f472d322dadc7f36.png">Figure 21</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  Locate the information in the Small UAS database.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Refer to the Military Operations Directory.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="true">
                  Contact Flight Service
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 26, area 2.) While monitoring the Cooperstown CTAF you hear an aircraft announce that they are left base to RWY 31. Where would the aircraft be relative to the runway?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_26/main-23f81c5aa1fa0a31c0bc01f38eda96971578c77425a661434cb9515d4782e96a.png">Figure 26</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_26/area_2-48e97a9dcef1f00fe6791c0cbf6a9cf0aedae4c025f8b8ad696b852cac38eb37.png">Figure 26 - Area 2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  The aircraft is East.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  The aircraft is North.
                </label>

        <h1>Questions 76&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;80</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>

      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>When operating near an uncontrolled airport, which frequency should the remote-pilot use to monitor air traffic?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="true">
                  CTAF
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  UNICOM
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="false">
                  AWOS
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which basic flight maneuver increases the load factor on an airplane as compared to straight-and-level flight?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  Climbs
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">

                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  Turns
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20.) How would a remote PIC &quot;CHECK NOTAMS&quot; as noted in the CAUTION box regarding the unmarked balloon?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>

        <h1>Questions 86&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;90</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the one common factor which affects most preventable accidents?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Mechanical malfunction
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Structural failure
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Human error
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the antidote when a pilot has a hazardous attitude, such as Resignation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  I am not helpless
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Someone else is responsible
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  What is the use
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20, area 6) What does the dashed magenta line East of Area 6 indicate?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="true">
                  Magnetic variation
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  Military operation area (MOA)
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  Class E starting at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 20 area 4.) What hazards to aircraft may exist in restricted areas such as R-5302B?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">

                </label>

                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">

                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  High volume of pilot training or an unusual type of aerial activity.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 91&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;95</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the purpose of the rudder on an airplane?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  To control roll
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  To control overbanking tendency
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  To control yaw
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You have received an outlook briefing from flight service through 1800wxbrief.com. The briefing indicates you can expect a low-level temperature inversion with high relative humidity. What weather conditions would you expect?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="false">
                  Light wind shear, poor visibility, haze, and light rain.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Turbulent air, poor visibility, fog, low stratus type clouds, and showery precipitation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="true">
                  Smooth air, poor visibility, fog, haze, or low clouds.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Which technique should a pilot use to scan for traffic?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Concentrate on relative movement detected in the peripheral vision area.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">
                  Systematically focus on different segments of the sky for short intervals.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  Continuous sweeping of the windshield from right to left.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is a characteristic of stable air?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">
                  Stratiform clouds
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Unlimited visibility
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  Cumulus clouds
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 12.) What are the current conditions for Chicago Midway Airport (KMDW)?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_12/main-e6a3de88341124b9dd2787199ee97941ea91ed730d5ce57c6bdb08efeb34659f.png">Figure 12</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  Sky 700 feet overcast, visibility 1-1/2SM, rain.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  Sky 7000 feet overcast, visibility 1-1/2SM, heavy rain.
                </label>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 101&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;105</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>Safety is an important element for a remote pilot to consider prior to operating an unmanned aircraft system. To prevent the final &quot;link&quot; in the accident chain, a remote pilot must consider which methodology?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Crew Resource Management.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Safety Management System.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Risk Management.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 107, what is required to operate a small UA within 30 minutes after official sunset?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Use of anti-collision lights.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Must be operated in a rural area.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Use of a transponder.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>According to 14 CFR part 48, when must a person register a small UA with the Federal Aviation Administration?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  Only when the operator will be paid for commercial services.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="true">
                  All civilian small UAs weighing greater than .55 pounds must be registered regardless of its intended use.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="false">
                  When the small UA is used for any purpose other than as a model aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 59, area 2.) The chart shows a gray line with &quot;VR1667, VR1617, VR1638, and VR1668.&quot; Could this area present a hazard to the operations of a small UA?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_59/main-f021280437b9236349c9ba72c050c72e0d59f489fa515f3ef34fe3a157881652.png">Figure 59</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_59/area_2-6ecded07a7ca4a227b9109944258821c96dd595b74439ab7b1bbc2f1d91216df.png">Figure 59 - Area 2</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="false">
                  No, all operations will be above 400 feet.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="true">
                  Yes, this is a Military Training Route from 1,500 feet AGL and below.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  Yes, the defined route provides traffic separation to manned aircraft.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>What is the antidote when a pilot has a hazardous attitude, such as Antiauthority?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="false">
                  Rules do not apply to this situation
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  I know what I am doing
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="true">
                  Follow the rules
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
        <div class="row">
          <div class="col-sm-8 col-sm-offset-2">

          </div>

          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 15) In the TAF for KMEM, what does SHRA stand for?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_15/main-9a47406eb4502bdf2bf63d153970e04c9c9375c955f1fc5f54031e38e2395bad.png">Figure 15</a></li>
              </ul>

      <div class="text-center section-header" id="faa_header">
        <h1>Questions 121&nbsp;&#8209;&nbsp;125</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>
      <form id="faa_quiz" data-questions="5">
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>If an unstable air mass is forced upward, what type clouds can be expected?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with considerable associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Stratus clouds with little vertical development.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Clouds with considerable vertical development and associated turbulence.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to Figure 20, area 6) What does the dashed magenta line East of Area 6 indicate?</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_20/main-7bb39947fef2e22d315ec0cc555cad991fa39b6782cfd7875796894340f3ae68.png">Figure 20</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_0" value="true">
                  Magnetic variation
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_1" value="false">
                  Military operation area (MOA)
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_1" id="question_1_answer_2" value="false">
                  Class E starting at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>(Refer to figure 25, area 4.) The floor of Class B airspace overlying Hicks Airport (T67) north-northwest of Fort Worth Meacham Field is</h3>
              <ul class="nav nav-pills">
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/figure_25/main-57bc6a20997504c7dfe6d1e894e7811561453c502faadd4248a5f29a8ea0c65e.png">Figure 25</a></li>
                  <li role="presentation"><a href="#" data-toggle="modal" data-target="#faa_modal" data-path="/assets/faa/practice_test/sectional_legend-cb94b2493a47391b96791f85a9e4b6f365b14707eef1858412d46b2422fba0b0.png">Sectional Legend</a></li>
              </ul>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_0" value="false">
                  at the surface
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_1" value="false">
                  3,200 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_2" id="question_2_answer_2" value="true">
                  4,000 feet MSL
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>To avoid a possible collision with a manned airplane, you estimate that your small UA climbed to an altitude greater than 600 feet AGL. To whom must you report the deviation?</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_0" value="true">
                  The FAA, upon request.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_1" value="false">
                  Air Traffic Control.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_3" id="question_3_answer_2" value="false">
                  The National Transportation Safety Board.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>You are a remote pilot for a co-op energy service provider. You are to use your UA to inspect power lines in a remote area 15 hours away from your home office. After the drive, fatigue impacts your abilities to complete your assignment on time. Fatigue can be recognized</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_0" value="true">
                  as being in an impaired state.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_1" value="false">
                  by an ability to overcome sleep deprivation.
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_4" id="question_4_answer_2" value="false">
                  easily by an experienced pilot.
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>

        <h1>Question 126</h1>
        <h2 class="status vanish">PLACEHOLDER</h2>
      </div>

          <div class="form-group question">
            <h3>The FAA may approve your application for a waiver of provisions in part 107 only when it has been determined that the proposed operation</h3>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_0" value="false">
                  Involves public aircraft or air carrier operations
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_1" value="false">
                  Will be conducted outside the United-States
                </label>
              </div>
              <div class="radio">
                <label>
                  <input type="radio" name="question_0" id="question_0_answer_2" value="true">
                  Can be safely conducted under the terms of that certificate of waiver
                </label>
              </div>
          </div>
